Grand Prix Trials Decklists
===========================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on April 18, 2015 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20170709072651im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/themes/wiz_mtg/images/global/generic-avatar-150.png)
By Olle Rade










As always, on the Friday before a Grand Prix there are last chance Grand Prix Trials offering byes for the following day's event. Here, at Grand Prix Krak처w, an impressive 37 standard trials took place last night, and 37 lucky winner earned their byes for the main event this morning. We took the time to give you all of the decklists.
